< review>
Loma Linda seems to be blessed with about two Thai restaurant every block. When yet another Thai restaurant popped up next to A Dong I didn‚Äôt even give it a second look. A couple years later and the restaurant changed its name and changed from serving small $5 plates to serving dishes like every other Thai restaurant. The food and service are great, and I was able to try the pad Thai, pat see ew, and parang curry. Classic flavors and competitive prices.<//review>

< Review>
I ordered Pad Thai when I went there the other day. I remember another time at another Thai restaurant in Redlands I had ordered Pad Thai and they went heavy on the fish sauce, and I couldn't finish it, it was not appetizing. So I decided to customize this order and told them to put very little to no fish sauce, and you know what? It was bomb. I would definitely come back for that order alone, but I will be coming back and trying other food items in their menu. The ambience is actually nice, humble but with a touch of class. I would definitely recommend anyone to give this place a try.< /Review>

<text>I'm an out of stater who travels to Los Angeles quite often .  I've been trying the local scene in regards to tacos and I tried my first three spots: El Ruso, Tacos 1986 downtown and Sonora town LA downtown.  I have to tell you, just based on the hype and the beautiful IGs,  I was slightly disappointed.  El Ruso was slightly better though and worth a shot.  Here's the pros and one major con

Pros: meat was well seasoned.  Better taste than the other two spots.  Tortillas were absolutely on point.  These are the thinner hand rolled variety that beautifully hold together its content.  Everything fresh made.  Service was friendly.

Con:. I hate fatty meat.  Forgive me if as an out of towner I may not understand the regional differences in a cut of meat but this tasted like it was closer to a ribeye which gave it phenomenal taste but a very chewy texture.  Honestly the only time a fattier cut of meat has worked for me is when it has been very thinned cut.  If you like your asada meat a bit on the fattier side then this place deserves the full 5 stars.<//text><Pics>None< /Pics>< Resp>
None< /Resp>

< Text>
I met Dr Cyrus Ezzati recently and I can sum up my experience by saying I wish I had met him a number of years ago. The office is fully compliant with everything one would expect in the COVID-19 era. You call as you wait outside the door until you are asked to enter for a temperature check and a short set of questions before you are escorted to a treatment room. You rinse with a hydrogen peroxide solution before your treatment. Dr Ezzati is knowledgeable, compassionate, attentive and skilled. He explains everything he is doing. While he has an assistant who does polishing and flossing, he performs dental cleanings himself. In my case, he expertly replaced a filling that had fallen out and replaced a crown that had failed, both of which were the work of other dentists. He does not recommend procedures that are unnecessary to boost profits. He easily resolved a problem that I have put up with for several years despite bringing it to the attention of other dentists.</Text>

<Review>Long Covid and infection burst a tooth. During the pandemic, many dentists were closed, but SmileSF was taking patients and had good reviews. The diagnosis was to address a variety of issues to give me the best chance of success with a crown on the broken tooth: Gum treatment was needed to clear infection, home care would be required to heal the gums. Next, the broken tooth was flanked by two teeth with old fillings, so those fillings were ready to be replaced, and the best time to do it would be during the clean out and installation of the new crown. I could understand it would be dicey dealing with either of those fillings later. So over the last 6 weeks I've had all this work done. The bonus is that my Long Covid episodes (which had escalated during the few weeks before my tooth burst) have subsided a great deal. Causation or correlation? Who knows? Long Covid is a mystery at this point. But many of us who had Covid-19 are having a variety of dental problems. SmileSF is practicing good protocols to keep them and we safe from re-infection. If you are cohort 2 (as I am) and episodes are increasing, checking for infection of your gums and teeth might be worthwhile. This office is struggling a bit with the Pandemic protocols, as everyone is. But they are fully equipped and careful. I would recommend Dr. Farah Sefidvash.</Review><time>1618508178643<//time><GmapID>0x808580d05b871f49:0x4d84d3bf645b69ce</GmapID><Response>None</Response>< user_id>

< Review>
THIS. IS. THE. BEST. PLACE. EVER!

This place never disappoints.

SCRATCH THAT.

The only time this place has disappointed me is when it's been CLOSED.

My go-to meal is the chicken combo which normally comes with, shredded chicken, beans, rice, radishes, tortillas, and - if wanted - onions,  and cilantro. Lately, I've been asking for the combos just with the chicken in whole pieces with no beans and double rice. See the Plato de Pollo pic below.

By the way... I am so thankful that I will NEVER have to admit to my late grandfather that I've found a roast chicken that tastes better than his! It is so moist, tender, and flavorful!

And the rice?!?!?!?! Praise him! If I'm running errands, I'll stop in just for an 8 oz. cup - only $2, yall!

Oh, yeah! The combos come with a fountain drink, but only if you

WEAR. A. MASK!</Review>

In my review of the El Toro Bravo tortilleria, I gave it a "4" for the food and service but dinged it for the relatively drab location.  Enter their new restaurant a few blocks down the street, which actually has the vibrance that the other location lacks while maintaining the same commitment to service and delicious food.  I'm a hefty dude, and even I get stopped in my tracks by the food portions they offer here and often take home the rest for seconds.  If you get a combo plate (asada, pollo, or carnitas), make sure you buy a bag of chips to go with it - Just makes the experience even better.< /review>

We offer a Basic program which offers all the necessities to obtain a Class "A" license, this course is guaranteed until you pass at The DMV. Our Basic course is what we offer at a promotional price for our Facebook friends and followers. In addition to the basic program we offer an upgraded course which will help enhance your knowledge when in the transportation industry. With this upgrade you will receive all the endorsements and a 160 hour certificate of completion and after working alongside the transportation industry for so long we are aware that companies favor applicants with more experience. < text>
Seriously a hidden gem for brunch! The brunch menu is more reasonably priced in my opinion and the portions are huge! High quality comfort food (we had the Spare Rib Tacos and the Crab Cake Benedict). No wait for a table inside, and I love the ambience - soft lit lamps and rich leather booths give a warm and cozy feel, perfect for 2 or smaller groups. The service is consistently excellent - attentive but not imposing. I also LOVE that parking is FREE and so easy to get in the Macy's structure behind the building, but valet is also available. I'm excited to come back and try their Happy Hour menu at some point!<//text>

< username>
Robert Brooks<//username>
< time>
1508929532620<//time>
<rate>4</rate>< Text>
Nice lighting, convivial atmosphere, and attentive staff. Paul Martin's sits amid a bustling Pasadena Mall area and the outdoor seating is nice in the evening which the traffic dies down.

Emelina was our server and was friendly and knowledgeable. Expos were unobtrusive and effective.

Let me here add a note about sequencing and timing: this restaurant had it down - bread arrived quickly and was crunchy-hot with flavorful butter. Salads soon after, and then the appetizers, all as if choreographed. Paul Martin's had it together this night.

The salad was as fresh as it possibly have been, with genuinely healthy plants such as red leaf and arugula and popping cold fresh tiny tomatoes.

Evening winner: the Pacific shrimp cocktail were like small lobsters with a meaty, fresh bite. The sauce itself had plenty of horseradish, giving this dish a potent one-two punch. Expensive and worth it. Runner up: fried shrimp appetizer with a blandish sauce (use instead the sauce that comes with the shrimp cocktail).

The iced tea had zero bitterness and stood on its own with no need for sweetener. Lots of lemon and lime were asked for and received.

Minor nits making this four stars instead of five: The entre was good but not great: ribeye steak was cooked to perfection, with a seared crust, but not on the beef quality level of the better steakhouses, being just a hint tough. The ubiquitous-standard mashed potatoes were salty-buttery and had a nice, firm consistency, but I would have ordered some satiny potatoes au gratin or better yet the crackling, fat onion rings - if this restaurant had any, which it does not :(

And finally the bill: A split entre, two appetizers, and two iced teas: $120 drive out. Well, this *is* Los Angeles. And Pasadena at that.< /Text>

<text>Came in with mild expectations, but left a true fan! As we walked through the big heavy doors and into contemporary surroundings, we were greeted by a friendly server. Inexplicably, while we were being seated, an restaurant employee broke a wine glass while rearranging the items on our big round table. The clean up was not the most thorough with tiny shards of glass still present and the employee did not seem very apologetic. We politely requested that they look over the table again and finally the rest of the glass was removed and the dinnerware and silverware all replaced with new sets.
Being a Monday, our party decided to go for their "Wine Dinner for Two" all day special. You get a selected bottle of wine, two field green salads, and two entrees of choice. I thought this was a great deal for $50! I came during the first week of the new year, however, the price has since then been raised to $60.
I ordered the "Brick" Chicken and it was appropriately juicy and tender. The sides were tasty as well. I will be back to try their filet mignon and/or other red meat options. Before we left, the manager personally came to apologize for the trouble caused by the broken wine glass and graciously gave us a discount as well! That was most definitely a pleasant surprise.< /text></record></dataset><record>
